Introduction

The API documentation for Bookshelves to use endpoints with another app.

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Base URL

http://localhost:8000

Authenticating requests

Authenticate requests to this API's endpoints by sending an Authorization header with the value "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}".

All authenticated endpoints are marked with a requires authentication badge in the documentation below.

You can retrieve your token by visiting your dashboard and clicking Generate API token.

Laravel Sanctum

http://localhost:8000/sanctum/csrf-cookie

Account

GET Current user.

requires authentication

Route name: api.v1.profile

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/profile" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/profile"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/profile',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Authorization' => 'Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}',
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Example response (500):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
vary: Origin

    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/authors"
);

const params = {
    "perPage": "5",
    "page": "1",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/authors',

            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',

GET List books.

WITH PAGINATION

Get all Books ordered by title & serie_title.

Route name: api.v1.books.index

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/books?filter[languages]=en%2Cfr&sort=title_sort&perPage=5&page=1" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/books"
);

const params = {
    "filter[languages]": "en,fr",
    "sort": "title_sort",
    "perPage": "5",
    "page": "1",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/books',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'query' => [
            'filter[languages]'=> 'en,fr',
            'sort'=> 'title_sort',
            'perPage'=> '5',
            'page'=> '1',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Request      

GET api/v1/books

Query Parameters

filter[languages]  string optional  

Filter by language, meta.slug from languages' list, null by default.

sort  string optional  

Sorting title_sort by default, available: title, title_sort, date, created_at, you can use - before parameter to reverse like -title_sort.

perPage  int optional  

Number of entities to return in a page.

page  int optional  

Page number to return, 1 by default

Response

Response Fields

data  object[]  

List of books.

links  object  

Links to get other pages.

meta  object  

Metadata about pagination.

    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/books/delaney-joseph/lerreur-de-lepouvanteur-fr"
);

    "Content-Type": "application/json",

};

    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
    ]
);

Request      

GET api/v1/books/{author_slug}/{book_slug}

URL Parameters

author_slug  string  

slug of author in meta.author books' list, in case of multiple authors, default author is selected so you need to refer to books' list and not authors' list, example: delaney-joseph

book_slug  string  

slug of book in meta.slug books' list, example: lerreur-de-lepouvanteur-fr

GET Book collection related entries.

WITH PAGINATION

Get all Series/Books related to selected Book from Tag/Genre.

Route name: api.v1.books.related

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/books/related/hobb-robin/le-fils-rejete-fr?perPage=5&page=1" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/books/related/hobb-robin/le-fils-rejete-fr"
);

const params = {
    "perPage": "5",
    "page": "1",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/books/related/hobb-robin/le-fils-rejete-fr',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'query' => [
            'perPage'=> '5',
            'page'=> '1',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

    --header "Accept: application/json"

};

}).then(response => response.json());

);

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/languages" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/languages"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/languages',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

GET Count.

Get count of entities for a selected collection. Available for Book, Serie and Author.

Route name: api.v1.count

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/count?entities=author%2Cbook%2Cserie&languages=fr%2Cen" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/count"
);

const params = {
    "entities": "author,book,serie",
    "languages": "fr,en",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/count',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'query' => [
            'entities'=> 'author,book,serie',
            'languages'=> 'fr,en',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

POST Send submission.

Route name: api.v1.submission.send

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/submission" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"name\": \"temporibus\",
    \"email\": \"ayla84@example.net\",
    \"honeypot\": false,
    \"message\": \"wlmcecyqmjqx\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/submission"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "name": "temporibus",
    "email": "ayla84@example.net",
    "honeypot": false,
    "message": "wlmcecyqmjqx"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->post(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/submission',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'json' => [
            'name' => 'temporibus',
            'email' => 'ayla84@example.net',
            'honeypot' => false,
            'message' => 'wlmcecyqmjqx',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Search

GET Search.

Search full-text into authors, books & series.

Route name: api.v1.search.index

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/search?q=cantos+d%27hyperion" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/search"
);

const params = {
    "q": "cantos d'hyperion",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/search',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'query' => [
            'q'=> 'cantos d'hyperion',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Serie

Endpoint to get Series data.

GET List series.

WITH PAGINATION

Get all series ordered by title & serie_title.

Route name: api.v1.series.index

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series?filter[languages]=en%2Cfr&perPage=5&page=1" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series"
);

const params = {
    "filter[languages]": "en,fr",
    "perPage": "5",
    "page": "1",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'query' => [
            'filter[languages]'=> 'en,fr',
            'perPage'=> '5',
            'page'=> '1',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();

Request      

GET api/v1/series/{author_slug}/{serie_slug}

URL Parameters

author_slug  string  

slug of author in meta.author series' list, in case of multiple authors, default author is selected so you need to refer to series' list and not authors' list, example: bottero-pierre

serie_slug  string  

slug of serie in meta.slug series' list, example: lautre-fr

GET Book collection of Serie.

Books list from one Serie, find by slug.

Route name: api.v1.series.show.books

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series/books/lore-pittacus/les-loriens-fr?perPage=5&page=1" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series/books/lore-pittacus/les-loriens-fr"
);

const params = {
    "perPage": "5",
    "page": "1",
};

    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series/books/lore-pittacus/les-loriens-fr',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'query' => [
            'perPage'=> '5',
            'page'=> '1',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Request      

GET api/v1/series/books/{author_slug}/{serie_slug}

URL Parameters

author_slug  string  

slug of author in meta.author series' list, in case of multiple authors, default author is selected so you need to refer to series' list and not authors' list, example: lore-pittacus

serie_slug  string  

slug of serie in meta.slug series' list, example: les-loriens-fr

Query Parameters

perPage  int optional  

Number of entities to return in a page.

page  int optional  

Page number to return, 1 by default

GET Book collection of Serie (from volume).

Books list from one Serie, find by slug from volume and limited to 10 results.

Route name: api.v1.series.current

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series/books/1/nicholson-william/le-vent-de-feu-fr" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series/books/1/nicholson-william/le-vent-de-feu-fr"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series/books/1/nicholson-william/le-vent-de-feu-fr',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));
